| Following material is intended for Biblical Studies work.
| But DBT does not presently support Unicode beyond U+FFFF.
| Characters import as Korean without this support.
| A reasonably trivial modification to chi/chuds.c and
| dbt/unimap.cpp could resolve the limitation that prevents
| us reading these mappings on import.
